Grand Prix Trial Winners' Decklists
===================================



 Posted in [GRAND PRIX PRAGUE 2016](/en/events/coverage/gppra16)
 on June 11, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/henke_author.jpg)
By Tobi Henke











As is tradition, Friday gave players their last chance to earn byes for today's main event: by going 5-0 in a 32-player single-elimination Grand Prix Trial. Their last chance and our first, that is, to get a good look at the decks which we should expect to see more of over the course of the weekend. So let's do that, let's get a good look!







#### Sami Häggkvist, Grand Prix Trial Winner


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
